Chamber of Commerce Sends Seal of Silk Products to the Ministry of Finance 130

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing yesterday, saying, "To the esteemed Ministry of Finance in Nanjing: On the 27th of this month, the Motor and Silk Weaving Factory Association of this city stated in a letter that, in order to assist the government in carrying out anti-smuggling and to maintain the sales of legitimate goods, the association will conduct identification of silk fabrics produced by members starting from October 1st, and affix a stamp on both ends of the silk to prove it. Currently, the products of members, whether old or new, have been stamped at the same time, and it is expected that all procedures will be completed before the 3rd of October, so that starting from November 1st, all silk fabrics produced by members will have the stamp of the association to prove it. If there are any silk fabrics that have not been stamped, it means that they have not been subjected to identification procedures, and the association will no longer provide proof. In this way, when the products of members are transported and sold to the interior, the anti-smuggling agencies along the way can easily identify them at both ends of the silk, so that legitimate domestic products can have the opportunity to be transported and sold conveniently. In addition to submitting two copies of the association's silk fabric identification rules, we are also sending two copies of the seal of the silk fabric certification stamp affixed to both ends of the silk for your review and approval. Please forward them to the Ministry of Finance and order the anti-smuggling agencies in various provinces and cities to verify this seal when inspecting the products of the Shanghai Silk Weaving Factory, and allow them to be released with the transport or distribution license to prove it, and to facilitate transportation and sales. To the meeting, the association conducts identification procedures for the products of the entire city's silk weaving factory colleagues, dividing them into four categories: silk fabrics, silk interwoven fabrics, rayon fabrics, and rayon interwoven fabrics. All goods identified by the association are stamped with the name of the product at both ends of the piece to distinguish them. It is for the purpose of assisting anti-smuggling personnel in identifying silk fabrics and maintaining the transportation and sales of domestic silk. It is beneficial to both commercial inspection and administration. We are sending the original silk fabric identification rules and a copy of the silk fabric certification seal for your Ministry's review and approval. It is publicly convenient to order the anti-smuggling agencies in various places to pay attention to it. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce expresses its gratitude."

Municipal Land Bureau Stipulates Procedures for People's Petitions 132

Xu Fu, the Director of the Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau, has stipulated specific procedures for the documents used in people's petitions, as the documents used are not consistent. The procedures were announced yesterday for public knowledge. The procedures are summarized as follows, totaling three items: A. People requesting matters from the bureau must use the current star-shaped paper, and write clearly and legibly. If there are matters related to property rights disputes, an additional copy should be prepared. B. The name should be signed or sealed below. C. The following petitions must be sealed by the shop guarantor: (1) Request to stop measurement and certification. (2) Acknowledge boundaries (regarding property dispute cases). (3) Report municipal public land. (4) Property rights disputes. (5) Request for re-issuance of lost single receipts, drawings, and land certificates. (6) Request to stop transfer and mortgage. (7) Request for reconciliation and cancellation of the case, limited to cases where there is no reconciliation record or judgment. (8) Request to increase or stop increasing the tax. (9) Change of address. If there is a seal stored in the bureau, no shop guarantor is required. (10) Accusation events.

Guangdong Shipping Merchants Request Cancellation of Annual and Seasonal Fees for Ferryboats and Electric Boats 136

Guangdong shipping merchants are seeking the cancellation of the annual and seasonal fees for ferryboats and electric boats in the province. The Shipping Association convened a meeting and recommended Chairman Xie Zhongchi to go to Beijing to petition. Mr. Xie has already left Guangdong and arrived in Shanghai and will go to Beijing within days to present everything to the relevant ministries and commissions of the Central Government. According to reporters, the fees have been collected by the Port Authority for a long time. Shipping merchants have repeatedly requested cancellation in the past, but it has not been approved. Now, since the establishment of the Guangdong Bureau, the Ministry has established a Maritime Affairs Bureau to handle maritime affairs, and the Department of Construction has established a Shipping Administration Bureau to preside over the collection. Shipping merchants believe that the amount of the tax is not stipulated in the maritime regulations. At a time when national political orders are unified, it seems inappropriate to have such a tax that is like an excessive miscellaneous tax. Therefore, they deeply hope that the Central Government will consider the people's difficulties and order the abolition of the tax to benefit shipping merchants. It is also heard that the tax revenue of more than 200,000 yuan a year is only enough to cover the administrative expenses of tax collection. If it is abolished by order, it will have no impact on finance or construction.

Inventor Yang Ming Establishes Invention Research Organization 137

Seeking Membership from All Circles

Inventor Yang Ming has recently invented a method of extracting white sugar from flour and brown sugar. In order to enable research and investment from all circles, he has established the China Invention Research Institute. The invention process is described below:

Invention Process: In the summer of the 23rd year, Yang Ming felt that China's sugar industry was underdeveloped. The national business revenue each year reached more than 10 million yuan. In particular, the consumption of white sugar all relied on foreign goods, resulting in huge losses. Therefore, he used his academic knowledge to study how to extract white sugar from brown sugar and flour. The method is to first extract brown sugar to increase its sweetness by half of the original brown sugar, and then add flour and mix it to make flour sugar. Its use and sweetness are equal to white sugar, and its cost is half the market price of white sugar, which is of great importance to the people's food supply.

Establishment of Research Institute: Now, in order to expand research, Mr. Yang has specially established the China Invention Research Institute to provide services to the national industrial and commercial circles in terms of invention and research, and to assist in soliciting joint membership from all circles across the country. The methods are divided into five groups: (1) Economic Sponsorship Group, (2) Research Cooperation Group, (3) Contacts Group for All Circles, (4) Office Service Group, and (5) Auxiliary Learning Group.

Weaving Factory Employees Beat Gatekeeper Yesterday 141

Dagong News reports that workers Zhang Paxi, etc. from five silk weaving factories in this city, Baohua, Tiancheng, Yiyou, Yucun, and Yongfeng on Baoli South Road in Caojiadu, recently convened a meeting to organize the Third District Silk Weaving Industry Trade Union and have obtained a permit from the Municipal Party Department and are actively preparing for it. However, due to misunderstandings on the part of the capitalists, the Baohua Factory first laid off 12 worker representatives from the factory, including Zhang Boxi, Xu Housheng, Huang Heqin, Zhu Shengrong, Zhou Ju'e, Zhou Xian'e, Zhang Yuzhen, and Shen Cuixian, on the grounds of sluggish production. At the same time, Tiancheng Factory also dismissed four worker representatives, and Yiyou Factory dismissed 16 people, which aroused public indignation among the workers. At about 5 pm yesterday, Zhang Paxi and more than 30 of the laid-off workers first went to the Baohua Factory to request reinstatement. Because the factory owner Chen Bingjun was not present, they could not get what they wanted. Passing by the Yucun Factory, the workers in the factory heard the news and all rushed out to respond. Several gatekeepers and staff members of the factory immediately attacked the workers, and a mutual fight broke out between the two sides. The Caojiadu Public Security Bureau heard the news and immediately sent Inspector Zhao to lead more than 60 police officers to disperse the workers. As a result, several people, including Zhang Boxi, Xu Housheng, Qian Zhangxi, Zhang Jinhua, Zhang Hepeng, and Wang Lingfeng, were seriously injured, and more than 30 people, including Li Taohua, Shi Juan'er, Qian Cengyun, Qian Zhangfei, Qian Fenzhu, and Qian Shengzhu, were slightly injured. The injured workers involved in the incident have now been sent to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Foreign Merchant Steamer Runs Aground Repeatedly – New Channel Discovered in the Yangtze River – Jiangxin Steamer Has Found a New Waterway 144

Recent significant changes in the Yangtze River waterway, due to a sharp drop in water levels, have rendered several sections impassable for river transport. It has become necessary to find new channels to facilitate traffic. The Jiangxin, a steamer of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, recently entered port. A reporter visited the ship’s owner, Mr. Huang Youshi, to inquire about the Yangtze River’s water conditions and the search for new waterways. Mr. Huang explained in detail that the rapid and early retreat of the Yangtze River this year is rare in its history. When the ship set out from Hankou, the water level was measured at twenty-seven feet. Upon reaching a location below Datong, known as

Earth Bridge Lighthouse

the water level had dropped significantly, causing changes in the navigation route. A foreign merchant steamer, the Mareitta, loaded with cargo from Hankou bound for Shanghai, ran aground at Zhangjiagang, downstream of Jiujiang, due to the sharp drop in water levels. Despite strenuous efforts, the cargo was transshipped, and the vessel managed to escape the initial grounding. As it proceeded downstream towards the Earth Bridge Lighthouse waterway below Datong, where the customs authorities had erected a beacon to indicate the navigation path, an unexpected change in the waterway occurred. The Mareitta, sailing along the designated route at that location,

Ran Aground a Second Time

in the Earth Bridge Lighthouse waterway because the water level had dropped below twenty feet. Since the steamer required a draft of more than twenty-one feet, it became deeply mired in the shallows and could not extricate itself. An urgent telegram was sent to Shanghai requesting assistance. Jardine Matheson sent three of its largest tugboats and eight large iron barges to the scene, planning to first lighten the steamer by transferring its cargo before attempting to refloat it. The Jiangxin steamer passed by while the rescue operation was underway. To ensure safety, Mr. Huang did not dare to follow the original navigation route and instead sought a new path, finding a depth of thirty-one and a half feet on the outer circle, thereby safely passing through. Upon the ship’s arrival in Wuhu, Huang Youshi reported the situation to the Wuhu Customs, who agreed to

Relocate the Beacon

to prevent further mishaps to river steamers. Simultaneously, a notice would be issued to all vessels to use the outer circle. Unexpectedly, upon reaching the Jiaoshan section of the Yangtze River near Zhenjiang, another significant hazard was discovered. The Jiaoshan section is typically a thoroughfare for upstream and downstream river traffic, but its riverbed contains numerous reefs. Normally, the water is deep enough to pose no obstacle to navigation, and river steamers pay little attention to them. However, due to the significant drop in water levels, the reefs were now only ten feet below the surface, while Yangtze River steamers typically require a draft of eleven feet or more. Vessels passing through this area risked striking the reefs, which posed a severe danger. Upon assessing the situation, Captain Huang was greatly alarmed and quickly diverted the ship to the

Dagang Waterway

bypassing Jiaoshan on the right to avoid this extremely hazardous zone. After the Jiangxin steamer arrived in Shanghai yesterday, in the afternoon, Mr. Huang Youshi went to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to report on the Yangtze River channel’s water levels and changes. He requested that the company promptly inform all its Yangtze River steamers to use the Dagang route when navigating up and downstream past Jiaoshan to avoid colliding with the reefs, and to use the outer circle at the Earth Bridge Lighthouse for safety. Given the rapid drop in water levels, there is concern that within a month, the Yangtze River channel will follow in the footsteps of Changsha and become impassable. Yesterday, Shanghai received a telegram from Xiangdian stating that the water level above Lulin Tan in Changsha was only two feet, making it impossible for even larger barges to pass, and only small boats with a draft of just over one foot could carry cargo.

Shanghai National Protection and Disaster Relief Dharma Assembly – Inaugural Meeting of Sponsors Held Yesterday 146

The Shanghai National Protection and Disaster Relief Dharma Assembly, initiated and organized by prominent figures from various sectors in the city, convened an inaugural meeting of sponsors yesterday afternoon at 2 PM at the Buddhist Jingye Society. The meeting approved the articles of association. A reporter from the Huadong News Agency provides the following report:

Attendees

Present were Qu Wenliu, Guan Jiongzhi, Huang Hanzhi, Hui Yunpei, Zhou Shouliang, Ding Chaicen, Li Jingwei, Shen Binhan, Hu Yuanfu, Li Dachao, Jian Yujie, Yuan Ying, Yuan Chen, and others. Qu Wenliu was elected as the temporary chairman.

Fundraising Methods

Following the performance of customary rituals, Qu Wenliu first reported on the preparatory progress. Subsequently, the methods for raising funds were approved, including: (1) general donations, (2) offering prayers for longevity, (3) admission tickets, (4) vegetarian meals.

Articles of Association

(1) The purpose of this Dharma assembly is to promote Pure Land Buddhism and encourage compassion in order to protect the nation and relieve disasters. (2) The Dharma assembly is scheduled to commence on November 22, 25th year of the Republic, with the consecration of the altar at 8 PM on the preceding day, and will conclude on the 28th. The Dharma assembly will be held at the Buddhist Jingye Society. (3) The program of chanting, lectures, and other regulations within the Dharma assembly will be determined by the presiding Dharma master. (4) For the convenience of handling affairs, this Dharma assembly will establish an office responsible for planning assembly affairs, which will be terminated upon the conclusion of the assembly. (5) The directors of the office will be publicly elected by the sponsors’ meeting, who will then elect a director-general, a deputy director-general, and standing directors to oversee all affairs of the office. (6) The office will establish three groups: documentation, accounting, and general affairs, each with a chief secretary and several secretaries, appointed by the director-general. (7) All staff members of the office will serve in honorary positions and may, if necessary, temporarily employ personnel and provide stipends. (8) After the conclusion of the Dharma assembly, the office shall prepare a report of receipts and expenditures and distribute it to all donors for verification. (9) These articles of association will be implemented upon resolution by the sponsors’ meeting, and any unresolved matters may be amended by the standing directors’ meeting.

Origin of the Dharma Assembly

In the summer of this year, the Bodhi Society, the Buddhist Jingye Society, and benevolent believers from all walks of life initiated the Bingzi Disaster Relief Dharma Assembly. At that time, Han and Tibetan monks, both exoteric and esoteric Dharma masters, gathered in one place to preach the scriptures and practice the Dharma, benefiting sentient beings. It was a complete and extraordinary event. For months, various regions have experienced abundant harvests and the people have enjoyed their work. The participants deeply appreciate the Buddha’s compassion and are increasingly diligent. The Dharma gate is immeasurable, and they vow to follow their studies, requesting the turning of the Dharma wheel without fatigue. They considered that to eliminate the five defilements of this land, one must take Amitabha’s great vow as the principle, and to eliminate the three poisons of sentient beings, one must take Avalokitesvara’s great compassion as the foundation. However, Amitabha’s vows cannot be achieved without Avalokitesvara’s compassion, so the great compassion Dharma assembly must be widely promoted. Venerable Master Yin, a respected elder of our time, whose merits, practices, and vows are universally admired, has been cultivating the Tao in Wumen in recent years, practicing meditation in seclusion. Moved by the chaos in the world, his compassionate vows have become even stronger. The residents of this society, Qu Wenliu, Huang Hanzhi, and Guan Jiongzhi, and others, went to Suzhou to request him to propagate the Dharma. The Venerable Master, with great compassion, readily agreed. Therefore, on November 21, they will respectfully welcome the Dharma chariot to Shanghai to preside over the establishment of the great compassion Dharma assembly for seven days, while holding the Buddha’s name, dedicating the merit to protecting the country and relieving disasters, and speaking to the masses about the Pure Land Dharma, hoping that everyone will practice. This is truly a rare opportunity. They also invited Dharma Master Yuan Ying to lead the congregation in incense cultivation, adorning the congregation with incense light. The Avatamsaka Sutra initially taught Samantabhadra with the ten great vows, leading to the Amitabha Buddha in the Pure Land. The Universal Gate Chapter of the Lotus Sutra greatly extols the merits of reciting the name of Avalokitesvara. It is known that Amitabha and Avalokitesvara encompass the entire teachings of the Tathagata from beginning to end. If one can recite the name of Amitabha with one thought, then that one thought resonates with the compassion of the two sages. If one recites the name of Amitabha with every thought, then every thought resonates with the compassion of the virtuous sages. Pure thoughts follow one another, eliminating greed, anger, and delusion. If everyone is like this, then this world will become a Pure Land, the nation will be secure, and disasters will cease. It is hoped that all great benefactors will generate a Bodhi mind, rejoice in the merits, and jointly accomplish this adornment. This is the beginning.

Small Black Coal Revived in Coffin – Family Buried Him Alive Assuming He Was Dead – Rescued After Hearing Cries 147

Zhou Liu, a Jiangbei woman residing at No. 3408 Hart Road, gave birth to a son named Xiao Heitan (Small Black Coal) last year. A few days ago, Xiao Heitan suddenly fell ill. However, on the 26th of this month, Xiao Heitan passed away due to the severity of his illness despite medical treatment. The Zhou family then purchased a small coffin for the burial and hired someone to carry it out and abandon it in a wasteland on Maibai Road. Unexpectedly, around 8 AM the day before yesterday, Chinese Constable No. 2752 of the Putuo Road police station reported receiving information about a child crying inside a small coffin in the wasteland on Maibai Road. The constable went to investigate and confirmed the report. He immediately telegraphed the police station, which dispatched an ambulance to the scene, and the child was removed from the coffin. He was taken to Guangren Hospital, where it was confirmed that the child was not dead but was suffering from pneumonia and was admitted for treatment. Meanwhile, detectives were dispatched to identify the child’s family to investigate why they had abandoned the child, who was still alive. Zhou Liu and Zhou Jianguo were taken into custody by the police station. Yesterday morning, police lawyer Shi Yaotang prosecuted them in Special Court No. 1 for abandonment under Article 194 of the Criminal Code. When questioned, both defendants confessed that Xiao Heitan was their biological son and had indeed died a few days ago, so they placed him in a coffin and abandoned him in the wasteland, but they did not know how he had been revived. Judge Fu acquitted Zhou Liu and Zhou Jianguo in court, but they were each released on bail of 200 yuan pending appeal. The child will remain in Guangren Hospital for treatment.

Bullock's Unprecedented Feat 148

Drove from Shanghai to Tianjin – Journey Took Twelve Days

Mr. Bullock, an accountant at the Shanghai Chinese-Foreign Bank, drove his car north on the 11th of this month, passing through Hangzhou, Anqing, Kaifeng, and other places, and safely arrived in Tianjin on October 23rd. The defendant, Jiang Yuequan, hired lawyer Yuan Hanyun to appear in court and stated, "I went to Shaoxing to recover from an illness, which is why I only missed seeing her for two weeks. Otherwise, how could a young woman be supporting an old man?" The judge, noting that the two parties have already had many children together, suggested that they first try to reach a settlement outside of court, before delving into the details. Therefore, the hearing was postponed for further investigation.

Tang Liqing, Former Principal of Shaoyu Primary School, Embezzles 1,000 Yuan of School Funds; Representatives of the Association Sue 159

The Shaoxing Fellow-Townsmen Association in Shanghai founded a primary school in Shanghai to educate the children of Shaoxing. Tang Liqing was hired as the principal. The school's funding was subsidized annually by the Chinese Education Department of the Public Works Bureau with 2,000 yuan, divided into four installments. Tang was responsible for collecting the funds with a letter of introduction from the association's board of directors. It was not until the end of last year, when Tang left his position and a new principal was hired, that it was discovered that Tang had embezzled two installments of the subsidy, totaling 1,000 yuan. At that time, the directors of the association had a fellow-townsman relationship with Tang and considered the ties of kinship. They were reluctant to immediately pursue the matter legally and only warned him in the newspaper to quickly clear the debt to avoid losing his reputation. However, Tang has still ignored the matter. Therefore, the association decided to send officer Qian Youlan as a representative to file a criminal lawsuit against Tang with the First Special District Local Court for embezzlement. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng held a court hearing. The defendant, Tang Liqing, is currently missing and cannot be located. According to Qian Youlan, who appeared in court, after discovering Tang's fraudulent activities, he also stated that he did not know the defendant's whereabouts. Judge Huang stated that since the defendant's whereabouts are currently unknown, the case is difficult to proceed with and decided to temporarily suspend the trial, instructing the plaintiff to investigate the defendant's whereabouts and then, in the name of the association's chairman, submit a request for further summons.

Chamber of Commerce Writes to the French Municipal Council Requesting to Stop the Abuse of Confiscating Rickshaw Licenses 160

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the French Concession Municipal Council yesterday, stating: "To whom it may concern, On the 27th of this month, we received a letter from the Shanghai Rickshaw Industry Association, requesting that we urge the French Concession Municipal Council to stop the police from abusing the confiscation of rickshaw licenses in order to show compassion. The letter stated that the rickshaw pullers' daily business has been declining sharply in recent years due to the widespread availability of buses and trams, and the poor economic situation. Their situation is already extremely pitiful. However, the French Concession police department is strict and demanding with rickshaw pullers, often finding fault with them, resulting in frequent penalties of license confiscation. Each penalty costs 40 cents or 1 dollar, so that the rickshaw pullers' hard-earned income is often not enough to pay the fines. Those who cannot redeem their licenses immediately are often penalized double the amount after several months. Furthermore, each police officer regards the number of rickshaw licenses confiscated as a standard for measuring their performance. The more, the better. For example, the Mailan Police Station redeems licenses all day long, with rickshaw pullers coming and going in an endless stream, resembling a business operation. The authorities are completely focused on fines and do not care about the rickshaw pullers' difficult business. The association has heard and seen this and cannot bear to stand idly by. Therefore, we respectfully request that your council forward this matter to the French Concession Municipal Council to strictly prohibit this practice, and instruct all police stations not to arbitrarily confiscate licenses and to reduce the amount of the fines to show that the purpose is to improve traffic and not to collect fines, thereby reducing the suffering of rickshaw pullers, which is to cultivate the vitality of society." Based on this, the rickshaw pullers' operation in the concession, assuming there are any accidental violations of traffic regulations, the police officers do not ask whether there is any intention to violate the regulations, and generally confiscate the licenses. The redemption cost is no less than 40 to 50 cents. May I ask how much hard work does a rickshaw earn a day? Whenever the police confiscate the licenses, the rickshaw pullers beg with sad faces and tears, completely revealing a situation of being unable to afford the fines. In order to improve traffic, your bureau should also consider the lives of ordinary rickshaw pullers. We should respectfully request that you promptly inform the Military Affairs Department that in the future, rickshaw pullers, assuming they commit a police violation, should first be given a warning with a mark, and not immediately confiscate the license and send them for a fine, in order to show compassion. We sincerely hope you will consider this.

Impersonating Customs Officials in Fraud; Another Fraud Case Discovered; Using Deception to Obtain Rayon; Selling Price Only Half of Cost 161

Russians P. Bukneits and Chinese Tan Wenhu, Bao Jun, etc., were arrested by the police for impersonating customs officers to defraud Koreans Jia Jiong Bai and Li Xinkui of 13,000 yuan. The details of their case have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Pan Zhenyang continued the hearing in Criminal Court No. 9. Police lawyer Qian Xunjiu stated that it has been discovered that before October 5th of this year, Pi and others had defrauded Japanese Kasa Kawa Fujisaburo of the Zhongxing Foreign Firm at No. 182 Kunshan Road of 12,000 pounds of rayon worth 8,100 yuan. The fact is that the defendant Bao Jun usually had contacts with Kasa Kawa. In February of this year, Bao told Kasa that he had many connections with customs officials. If rayon was transported to Shanghai, only a small amount of customs duty needed to be paid. Bao also introduced Pi to Kasa. At that time, Kasa believed it to be true and shipped rayon worth 8,100 yuan from Japan. After the goods arrived in Shanghai, Pi and others used deception to make Kasa hand over the bill of lading to them for safekeeping. Afterwards, they took the goods out and sold them at a low price of 4,000 yuan. Now, due to the urgency of the case, many documents have not been translated yet. Therefore, he requested that the detention period be extended and the case be adjourned. Judge Pan interrogated Kasa Kawa and the defendants and ordered the case to be adjourned for further hearing.

Commander Yang Donates Funds to Continue Compiling the Ningguo County Gazetteer 165

Now Completed and Ready for Publication

The Ningguo County Gazetteer was revised during the Kangxi, Qianlong, and Daoguang dynasties of the former Qing Dynasty. However, the editions published during the Qianlong and Daoguang periods were destroyed during the Taiping Rebellion and no longer exist. The only extant edition is the one published during the Kangxi period, which is now over 200 years old and has not been revised since. Local historical documents are difficult to research. During the late Qing Dynasty and the Republic of China, there were repeated discussions about revising the gazetteer, but due to changes in personnel and the high cost, the resolutions were made but the book was never completed. Yang Xiaotian, a native of Ningguo County, is enthusiastic about local public welfare and has provided much financial assistance. Ningyang Park in the county was built with funds donated by Yang. Recently, Yang donated a large sum of money again, enabling the county gazetteer to be revised. The Ningguo County Government hired scholars Li Zhongcheng and Xu Yuntao to lead the project, and hired more than ten interviewers to collect and compile the information. The project took two years and is now completed. It has been handed over to the Hanwen Zhengkai Printing House on Wangping Street in Shanghai for printing. The printing is currently in progress. The gazetteer also includes a preface by the late master of Chinese studies, Mr. Zhang Taiyan. It is expected to be published this year. From now on, not only will the local historical documents of Ningguo County not be lost, but a portion of the anecdotes of Anhui Province can also be researched, which will further enhance local culture.

Borrowing Meat to Meet Market Demand Leads to Argument and Assault 173

Fang Xiaomao, a Ningbo native, is 24 years old and has a meat stall at the Hongkou vegetable market, with the certificate number 196. Yesterday morning around 6 a.m., he borrowed dozens of catties of fresh meat from his fellow stall owner Fang Awang (age 28) to meet market demand. Unexpectedly, an argument broke out between them, which then escalated into a fight. At that time, Fang Awang held a meat knife and stabbed Xiaomao in the chest, causing him to bleed profusely. Patrol officers nearby rushed to the scene and arrested the assailant Fang Awang on the spot, taking him to the Hongkou police station for detention. Issues of Appellate Correction 174

Lawyer Association Proposal

Shanghai Lawyers Association members Zheng Wentong, etc., stated that civil appeal cases often lack essential elements, resulting in their rejection. They proposed a remedy and suggested that the Lawyers Association submit it to the Ministry of Judicial Administration to allow the issuance of an order to all courts nationwide that whenever appeal cases lack essential elements, they should be ordered to be corrected first for remedy. The Association has submitted this case to a joint meeting of executive and supervisory committee members. After review by the assigned members, it was resolved to submit it to the Ministry of Judicial Administration and request that an order be issued to all county courts nationwide that whenever appeal cases lack essential elements, regardless of whether they are represented by a lawyer or drafted by a lawyer, the appellant should be ordered to correct them first for remedy. Yesterday, the Standing Committee submitted a document to the Ministry of Judicial Administration, requesting its adoption and the issuance of an order to all courts nationwide to comply.

Letters to the Editor 179

To the Editor: Upon reading the news item "Workers Engaging in Armed Fights Due to Carrying Goods" in the local news section of your esteemed newspaper on the 28th of this month, it was mentioned that "the old-school workers plan to support Xu Jintang, a standing committee member of the labor union, as their leader, hence the intense infighting," and so on. However, the standing director of our union is Comrade Tang Shanlin, not Xu Jintang. Furthermore, Xu Jintang is not listed on our union's membership roster. We believe this is a rumor. The unfortunate incident occurred because the workers suffered excessive oppression and exploitation of wages by the contractor Li Shibao. Therefore, our union petitioned the Social Affairs Bureau twice to convene a mediation. However, that Li Shibao disregarded everything, using force to oppress and dismiss all our union members, hiring seventy or eighty new workers to replace them, which led to this tragic event. This is truly regrettable. Besides reporting the situation to the Party and government authorities for investigation, we fear that the rumors are inaccurate. Therefore, we specially request your esteemed newspaper to correct this, fulfilling our public duty. Respectfully submitted to the Chief Editor of Shen Bao, Shanghai Fourth District Civil Ship Carrying Trade Union, October 28th.

To the Editor: Upon reading the news item in your esteemed newspaper about the tension between the two sides and the armed fight among fruit workers, we find it inconsistent with the facts. We hereby send this letter to your newspaper, requesting you to correct it as follows: (1) The fruit carrying workers employed by our company are all casual laborers, with no distinction between old and new factions. This unfortunate incident occurred due to casual laborers fighting over work. (2) The report in your newspaper stating that foreman Li Shibao frequently oppressed and exploited the workers' wages is absolutely untrue. Our company has never had the title of "foreman." The workers' wages are paid directly by each shop according to the amount of work done, so there is no possibility of wage exploitation. We earnestly request your esteemed newspaper to publish the aforementioned facts to correct public opinion. Respectfully submitted to Shen Bao, Shanghai Guang Bang Fruit Industry Lianyi Hall, October 28th.

Commercial News

Yarn and Cotton 181

Existing sales are sluggish. Although cotton yarn wants to rise, it still falls. November has already passed the 220-yuan mark.

The yarn market rose in the morning and fell in the afternoon, and the situation was very soft. This is because existing yarn sales are sluggish, and the cloth trade is also slack, causing market prices to fall. There is a lot of panic, and more people are cutting their losses. In fact, the previous surge was too violent, so this kind of reaction was expected. The November futures yarn has fallen sharply by 12.6 yuan from the peak on the 20th. If there are no unexpected changes, it may be stable for the time being. The key to the future still depends on whether actual sales improve.

Speculative yarn buyers are panicking and cutting their losses.

The pre-market opening for speculative yarn saw a slight improvement in sentiment due to the rebound in imported cotton. All months rose by one yuan. The second round of trading saw a slight drop. The third round of trading saw a sharp rise of four yuan in near-month Osaka Grade 3 yarn and two yuan in far-month yarn, boosting morale and causing a further rise of five or six jiao. By the time the market closed, news that yarn sales were sluggish and customer purchases were weak caused the market to decline, and all months rose by only three, six, nine jiao to one yuan and one jiao compared to the previous day's closing price. The afternoon opening saw sluggish spot yarn transactions and speculative buyers cutting their losses, causing a sudden surge in the decline. Near-term contracts fell by two yuan, and far-term contracts also fell by one and a half yuan. After the second round of trading, near-month contracts remained weak and broke through the 220-yuan mark. Far-month contracts were better. The spot yarn trade was too sluggish. As a result, November contracts fell by 2.6 yuan compared to the morning closing price, and far-term contracts fell by one to two yuan. It is recorded that Juxing sold 3,300 bales, Jinchang 1,550 bales, Zhenda 850 bales, Shenji 1,000 bales, Yicheng 1,400 bales, Hengyi 3,000 bales, Senkang 3,500 bales, and Changfeng 4,150 bales. Zhunyuda bought 2,200 bales, Minghua 1,850 bales, Fengtai 2,600 bales, Wangtai Yu 1,550 bales, Taichang 1,400 bales, Runkang 1,550 bales, Heyu 1,350 bales, Yu Chang 2,300 bales, Dachangcheng 1,200 bales, Jinkang 800 bales, and Dachang 850 bales. Piece Goods- Fine Twills Have Exceptionally High Market Prices 185

Yesterday's cotton cloth market was flat and weak. Speculative yarn and cotton once retreated, eventually trending downstream, making it difficult to boost morale, resulting in a stagnant cloth market. Profitable holders of goods continued to dump them at low prices. However, the sales performance of various customer routes was still good. Those in Shanghai who had placed orders for various cloths were particularly eager to pick up their spot goods. Factory production remained extremely tight, no less so than before. Therefore, the factories' attitudes remained quite calm. White goods, coarse cloth, and heavyweight goods remained scarce. Recently, small amounts of military uniforms have been added in various places, but there are no spot goods available to meet the demand, and the market remains firm. The supply of lightweight coarse cloth on the market has gradually increased, with slight inventory. However, the demand for 11-pound and 9-pound coarse cloth for jacket linings is increasing daily, and the market decline is also minimal. Recently, the market price of fine twills has been exceptionally high because the uniforms for civil training in various places this year all use dyed twill cloth. Therefore, the demand is huge, and the cost of soft fine cloth is also high (3 or 4 jiao per bolt). Yesterday, customer groups continued to ship goods in large quantities. Small amounts of new dyed goods were also sold, and prices were also stable. The ports of Changsha, Hankou, Anqing, Wuhu, and Jiujiang were the busiest, while the sales of goods to the southern routes of Guangdong, Yunnan, and Fujian were also smooth. Most of the goods shipped were pre-ordered, with only slight additions of fine and coarse cloth.

Domestic Woolen Fabrics Are in Particularly Strong Demand 186

Creating unprecedented new records.

A phenomenon after rural areas have improved

Yesterday's woolen fabric trade was very prosperous, and the trade association's trend was excellent. The supply of most domestic woolen fabrics could not meet the demand, resulting in prices rising one after another. Although the raw material of woolen yarn has risen sharply, the market progress this autumn, abundant agricultural harvests, lack of inventory in various ports, and increased purchasing power of customers are all major reasons. Therefore, if there are no changes in the current situation, the woolen fabric market should make greater progress. Yesterday, Dalong, Zhanghua plain serge, Zhanghua Renli uniform flannel, Xiexin straight tribute Western suit flannel all saw increases. Lianyi sold six or seven tenths without any goods. The briskness of the market can be said to be an unprecedented new record for domestic woolen fabrics.

Metals: Black Iron Sheets Suddenly Scarce 194

Japanese Continuously Searching Overseas, Futures Orders Possible Only After Five or Six Months

Black iron sheets (specifically, the sheets used for black-headed nails) are essential for products such as paint cans and ironware. However, previously, due to abundant inventories and continuous arrivals, the market trend was weak and lackluster, and standard quotations were also very soft, with each picul selling listlessly at 5.4 to 5.5 jiao. In recent days, overseas telegrams have indicated that this type of product has been purchased by Japan, and deliveries to China may only be possible for futures orders placed five to six months from now. This has caused panic among local manufacturers who need this product, leading to frantic searches. However, after a month of scouring the market, supplies have become scarce, causing prices to jump repeatedly. The price per picul has risen to 6.4 yuan. It is said that there are still no large quantities of spot goods available, and buyers from Hubei, Tianjin, Sichuan, and Jiangxi also inquired about the product yesterday, suggesting that the market situation is unlikely to ease in the short term.

Popular Lectures

Ferdinand Magellan (1470-1521) 198

— Shu Ying

－The First Explorer to Circumnavigate the World－

When we open a world map, we can see a very prominent strait at the southernmost tip of South America, called the Strait of Magellan. Magellan was originally a person's name, and using a person's name as the name of a strait, everyone who sees it will probably have some doubts and believe that this strait must have a history. Below, we will talk about the origin of this strait and the great explorer who discovered it.

Originally, people used to think that the Earth was not spherical. It was not until Columbus discovered the New World that it was proven that the Earth was indeed spherical. However, Columbus mistakenly believed that the New World he discovered was part of India. He imagined the Earth to be too small. He did not know that the island of San Salvador he discovered was another continent in the West, separated by a vast ocean. The other side of the ocean was India in the East.

However, what the Portuguese Magellan saw was different from Columbus. He believed that the place Columbus reached was definitely not the Orient. There must be a new continent between the Eastern and Western Hemispheres, blocking the way. To reach the Orient, one must pass through this new continent. Therefore, later, under this belief, coupled with his courage and spirit of exploration, Magellan began his life of exploration. Although he went through many twists and turns, and even lost his life in this exploration, he finally proved that his vision was correct, and it was his party that first completed the circumnavigation of the world.

As we mentioned above, Magellan was Portuguese, born in 1470 AD, twenty years younger than Columbus, so he was only twelve years old when Columbus reached the west coast of America. After growing up, he served as a volunteer in the Portuguese fleet, so he was particularly proficient in navigation, geography, and practical warfare. Later, due to various reasons, he left Portugal and served in the Spanish royal family. Soon, Magellan gained the trust of the King of Spain, who agreed to help him realize his ambition of exploration.

Magellan was overjoyed after receiving the help of the King of Spain. He led 250 people on five sailing ships and set off from Spain on September 20, 1519 AD. The two larger sailing ships were about 120 tons each, and the other three were smaller. After setting off, they traveled day and night, and finally reached the new continent of South America on November 29. The natives here saw Magellan and his team coming and regarded them as gods. They regarded the things they brought as treasures and exchanged livestock and all kinds of food for small bells, knives, iron axes, and so on.

They continued to travel south along the coast, passing through many places that no one had ever been to before. Later, because the weather turned bad, they had to temporarily stop advancing and spent the winter in a place called St. Julian Bay, thus extending the scheduled date. Magellan feared that the food supply would not be enough and that there would be danger in navigation later, so he decided to ration the food, stipulating the amount of food for each crew member. Unfortunately, some crew members were jealous of Magellan's achievements and deliberately made things difficult for him. His name was Cartagena. He led a part of the crew to oppose the distribution of food. Quite a few crew members were deceived by him and planned to divide into three ships and leave Magellan. Fortunately, Magellan discovered this dangerous plot in advance. With his extraordinary talents and means, he broke the conspiracy and suppressed the opposition to the distribution of food. After careful interrogation, many who were willing to repent were allowed to return to the ship. Only Cartagena and a few others still opposed and refused to repent, so when their ship set off, these people were left on the island, not allowed to return with them.

After the rebellion ended, Magellan ordered the ship to set sail again and continue southward. However, the coastline was endless, and there was no trace of the place they wanted to reach. But Magellan never despaired. He bravely moved forward and finally, on October 21, 1520, finished the coastline and discovered the strait. This is the Strait of Magellan that we see on the map. Magellan finally received this reward with a spirit of perseverance and hard work. At this time, the sailors were also overjoyed. Some even advised Magellan to turn back from now on, saying that since they had discovered the strait, they had already made a great contribution to the country. But Magellan still insisted on moving forward, passing through the strait, and the ship reached the vast ocean, the climate was mild, and the waves were calm. This is the Pacific Ocean. They thought that by passing through the Strait of Magellan, they would soon reach the Eastern Hemisphere, but they did not know that the ship had entered the ocean again. However, Magellan never lost heart and continued to sail. After another month or two, their food was exhausted, and the water was turbid. They were about to resort to gnawing on the canvas when, fortunately, the crew members were inspired by Magellan's heroic courage, and there was no fear or complaint. The five ships still bravely sailed forward. However, because life was too hard, and the water was not clean, more and more people died of illness every day, so they decided to rest on the island of Rateron. After a few days, they continued to move forward. In a few days, they reached the Philippine Islands. The Filipinos thought that they were all Eastern countries, but in fact, they came from Portugal and were travelers from Western countries, so it was further proven that the Earth is round.

Magellan's success was entirely due to his perseverance and indomitable will. He overcame all difficulties, even rationing food, which proves the saying that "where there is a will, there is a way." No matter who it is, as long as they have determination and can endure hardship, I think they will definitely achieve something.

However, unfortunately, although Magellan had such great achievements, opened a new record for traveling around the world, and became a great man with immortal fame in history, he later preached Christianity in the Philippines because of his belief in Jesus, which aroused the opposition of the natives. As a result of the natives' sabotage in various ways, he disregarded his own small number of people and decided to conquer the natives by force. He only relied on the fact that his weapons were better than those of the natives, so he boldly led more than sixty people to fight against more than a thousand natives. As a result, they were outnumbered and defeated by the natives. During the retreat, Magellan was finally wounded by a poisonous spear from the natives. Although Magellan also repelled dozens of natives, he was eventually killed by the natives because of the disparity in numbers. If this great explorer of the century had not preached, he would have been able to return to Spain safely with his companions. Later, his companions arrived safely in Spain on September 6, 1522, amidst a grand welcome. Although few were left, the cause of circumnavigating the world was thus successful.

The Fang Clan's Disaster in the "Jingnan Campaign" 199

— Shen Lu

Whenever a country is in turmoil, loyal ministers and martyrs will always emerge, sacrificing their lives for righteousness and inspiring the people and reviving the national soul. But the authorities always use high-pressure tactics to try to stop this fierce action, and the result is the development of all kinds of cruel tragedies.

Zhu Yuanzhang, the Taizu of the Ming Dynasty, rose up as a commoner, drove back the Hu people, and ruled China, which was also prosperous and the people lived in peace. It was not until May of the thirty-first year of Hongwu that Taizu contracted a serious illness. A month later, he died of illness. His will stated that the throne should be inherited by his嫡grandson Yunwen, because Yunwen was intelligent and filial, and the world had already turned to him, and it was customary to follow the嫡line. When the嫡son died, it was the嫡grandson's turn, so Yunwen immediately ascended the throne as instructed, and the following year was the first year of Jianwen. This was Emperor Hui.

At that time, Emperor Hui had an uncle named Di, who was naturally fierce and violent. Seeing that Emperor Hui's father had died early, he had the intention of usurping the throne. Taizu also knew his intentions, so he sent him to Beiping and made him the Prince of Yan, thinking that in this way, even if he had evil intentions, his power would be far away and could not be realized. Who knew that after the Prince of Yan went north, he trained his troops and dominated one side. Not long after Taizu died, he used the excuse of opposing Emperor Hui's advice to use Fang Xiaoru and others to change the official system, and under the guise of "Jingnan," he raised troops to invade the south.

The Prince of Yan fought all the way to Nanjing and entered the Jinchuan Gate directly. The capital was captured, and a fire broke out in the palace, killing many people. Emperor Hui's whereabouts were unknown. The Prince of Yan, fearing that the people would not submit, ordered the queen's remains to be obtained, prepared for burial with courtesy, and also said that Emperor Hui had died by self-immolation. He established himself as emperor, named Chengzu, which was in June of the fourth year of Jianwen. In July, Chengzu changed that year to the thirty-fifth year of Hongwu, abolished the new system, restored the old system, and the following year was the first year of Yongle. Chengzu thought at the time that doing so was in accordance with the will of heaven and the people, and he did not care about the criticism of later generations.

Here, let's talk about Mr. Fang Xiaoru again. He was from Ninghai County, Zhejiang Province. His father, Keqin, was a good official during the Hongwu period. Xiaoru was intelligent and different from others from a young age, and was known as "Little Hanzi." When he grew up, he had a dignified character and profound knowledge. Ming Taizu called him "Zhuangshi." The King of Shu Xian also hired him as a teacher for the世子, and named his书舍 "Zhengxue Lu." When Emperor Hui ascended the throne, he was summoned to be a侍讲, and all major policies were discussed with him before they were implemented.

After Chengzu usurped Emperor Hui's throne by violence, he listened to Yao Guangxiao's words, thinking that Fang Xiaoru was the seed of scholars in the world and could not be killed. Therefore, when Chengzu ascended the throne, he summoned him and ordered him to draft the诏文. Xiaoru was very sad and indignant because Emperor Hui was forced to commit suicide and the throne was usurped, so he wore filial piety clothes all over his body and cried to the palace. At that time, Chengzu comforted him: "Why is先生so sad? I am just learning from the Duke of Zhou to assist King Cheng!" Xiaoru said angrily after listening

"Where is King Cheng?"

"He burned himself to death."

"Then why not establish King Cheng's son?"

"The country depends entirely on the长君."

"Then why not establish King Cheng's brother?"

"This is Teng's family matter, don't you interfere,"

At this time, Chengzu became angry and taught his subordinates to hand over the笔墨纸札to Xiaoru, saying: "Shaowen must be drafted by先生!" Xiaoru thought that this was a matter of betraying great righteousness and could not be subdued by might, so he threw the pen on the ground, and cried and scolded: "... You can kill me, but I will not覃诏!" King Yan was unwilling to give up and said angrily: "How can you die so cheaply, I will also destroy your ten clans!" He forced him to write, Xiaoru knew that the situation was like a tiger on the road and could not be stopped. He simply wrote the four characters "Yan thief usurped the throne" and handed them up. Chengzu looked at them, and it was true that "anger rises from the heart, and evil grows from the胆." He immediately ordered the guards to arrest him and put him in prison. Later, he was tied to the market and beheaded together with Shangshu Qi Tai and Taichangqing Huang Zicheng. When Xiaoru was executed, he died with great courage and was not sad at all, and wrote a poem of绝命词:

"Heaven sends chaos, who knows the reason?

奸臣 gets his way, and the country is used like you.

Loyal ministers are angry, blood and tears are flowing,

Take this to seek殉, what else can you ask for?

Alas, alas, may you not allow me."

At that time, he was only forty-six years old.

His wife, Zheng Shi, and two sons - Zhongxian Zhongyu - all hanged themselves to death when they heard the news, and two daughters - Zhen and Shu - also committed suicide by throwing themselves into the Qinhuai River.

When Xiaoru's younger brother, Xiaoyou, was arrested and executed, Xiaoru saw him and couldn't help but feel sad and shed tears, but Xiaoyou chanted a jue句:

"Why does阿兄weep 澘澘?

Taking righteousness and becoming benevolence is here,

After the領表柱頭 for thousands of years,

The旅魂 still returns to 家山."

How tragic! There must be a brother if there is a brother, that's really right.

His friends and students were designated as "Fang's Party" by the authorities, and it is not known how many were遗謫or executed, such as Tong Bolü being transferred to Lulong, Zhang You's five brothers being sent to the border guards, Zheng Gongzhi, the assistant inspector of Shaanxi, and Lin Xiyou being sentenced to death, Lu Yuanzhi, the少卿of Taichang, and his brother Lu Yuanpu being滅家, and进士Zhang You and俞尹璋 also committed suicide because of this. ...

The decree of灭族 arrived at先生's hometown - Ninghai - and the Ninghai County authorities did not dare to neglect it. They quickly sent troops to search and arrest, which really made ghosts cry and gods howl, and chickens and dogs were not spared. A total of 827 people of his clan were killed one after another, and the corpses piled up into mountains and the blood flowed into rivers. No one dared to clean them up. At that time, there was a man named Ma Zitong, who, moved by righteousness and indignation, threw these corpses into a well and committed suicide by jumping into the well. Later, the water in this well was red for many days. During the Wanli period, Magistrate Wu Lai built a pavilion on this well and inscribed it with the four characters "义井忠泉." Now this Yijing Pavilion is still on Dajie Street in Ninghai City, and everyone who passes by expresses condolences and admiration.

At that time, anyone who hid Xiaoru's articles was sentenced to death. His fellow countryman, Mr. Zhang Pu, was reported by Yang Shan, the county序班of Ningbo, for collecting Fang's collection. Chengzu was very angry and arrested him. His younger brother, Zongjian, also followed him and cried and beat the "登闻鼓," willing to die and was also arrested. During the trial, Zhang Pu said. "Xiaoru was killed for being loyal to the country, and most of his articles praised the ways of the former kings and cannot be regarded as evil!" The judge passed these words to Chengzu, who became even more angry and immediately ordered him to be taken to the market and beheaded. Zhang Pu's face did not change when he was about to die, and he chanted poems calmly, and Zongjian also chanted poems in harmony. They were killed together. (The currently circulating collection of articles was copied and passed down by Wang Tú.)

Because everyone was afraid of the Party's disaster and was afraid of being implicated, no one dared to clean up Fang Xiaoru's remains. His表侄 Zheng Xun planned to take the remains to his hometown for burial with his student Wang Tú in Pujiang and Jinling, but was known by the authorities and was arrested and imprisoned. Later, because Chengzu accidentally thought of Wang Tú's grandfather, Wang Yi, who was a loyal minister of the former dynasty, he was specially pardoned, and Mr. Fang's remains were still hastily buried outside Jushimen in Nanjing, where he was executed.

When Fang's clan was滅族ed, everyone sighed that Fang's clan had no descendants and was about to be 절嗣. Fortunately, Xiaoru's second son Yi was hidden by Wei Tan, the former刑部尚齐邑尉, and thus passed down a lineage. Publishing Industry

Talking about Magazines 200

— Hu Xingzhi

－With Two Demands－

Books are the food for people to seek knowledge, and all modern people need them. Not to mention adults, even children need them, so the level of culture of a country can be judged by looking at the quality and quantity of its publications.

However, the scope of books is too broad, including specialized research books, school textbooks, and casual novels, etc., which cannot be fully discussed at one time. What I want to talk about now is magazines.

The so-called magazine actually encompasses everything. Because of its different nature, there are specialized ones, general ones, those that focus on literature and art, those that focus on economics or politics, and even those that are known for cartoons or曲线美. The various types are really a glimpse of the world.

But no matter how many forms there are and how complex the types are, they can be roughly divided into three categories: soft, hard, and a combination of hard and soft.

Those that generally focus on academic research are usually called hard, those that focus on leisure are called soft, and those that provide knowledge and have a recreational nature are called hard-soft publications. However, there are few absolutely hard ones, and the absolutely soft or hard-soft ones account for the majority.

In terms of the time of publication, there are two types: regular publications and irregular publications. Regular ones include annual publications, quarterly publications, bi-monthly publications, monthly publications, semi-monthly publications, weekly publications, etc. Most of the irregular ones are group publications of academic societies, and most of them are research-oriented.

In the past, magazines, especially during the turbulent revolutionary wave, often talked about politics, and most of them contained a nature of promotion and propaganda. Recently, politics has become slightly more stable, and the trend of academic research is more popular, so specialized research-oriented publications have slightly emerged, which cannot be said to be a gratifying phenomenon. In fact, it is also a necessary phenomenon.

However, the world situation is in a turbulent wave, and international changes are changing rapidly, so publications that study international situations are still very developed, which is also promoted by the times.

Although academic knowledge is needed by everyone, the education system under capitalism deprives the poor of the right to enjoy medicine and reading. In response to this need, there are various magazines that help self-study, such as "Reading Youth" and "Reading Monthly."

The world economy is in recession, rural areas are bankrupt, and the number of unemployed people in society is increasing day by day, so people want to find a sideline to make a living, so there are so-called "Rural Sideline Monthly" and "Chicken Raising Magazine," etc.

Young people are wandering on the wrong path and mostly like to read literary works as spiritual comfort. The various novels and magazines published by the Creation Society in the past have won the welcome of many young people, which is clear proof. Therefore, literary publications are still on the road to prosperity and development, such as "Writer," "Literary Artist," "Midstream," "Translation," and "Literature" and "Literary Quarterly," etc., which seem to be emerging one after another.

There are also publications that are aimed at people, such as "Middle School Student" published by Kaiming, "Youth Circle" published by Beixin, and "Youth Monthly" published by Zhengzhong, which are specifically for middle school students; "Education Magazine," "Education Circle," and "Elementary Education," etc., which are specifically for the education sector; and those for elementary school students are even more numerous, but most of them focus on both pictures and texts.

Recently, there have been so-called humorous magazines. Frankly speaking, these humorous magazines also have their own merits, but humor should not be taken as a serious matter. "Cosmic Wind" and "Analects" are representatives of this type of magazine.

From the branch of humor, combining revolutionary anecdotes and talking about literature and history, Yijing is well-known for its sales.

People either go upward or downward, but going upward is like sailing against the current, which cannot be done without great certainty, so it is easy to go downward. Carnal sensuality is the easiest to seduce people; laughing and scolding are the easiest to win people's favor, so in order to cater to the preferences of the times, there are various boring publications. Full of curvy sensuality, nude images of women, "The Unofficial Biography of Mr. Wang," "Cartoon Circle," "Cartoon World," etc., are endless. This is also the psychology of seeking comfort in boredom. Those who are in tune with this include dance halls on the sea with five tickets for one yuan, girl singing and dancing troupes, massage parlors, and indescribable toys, etc.

Hard publications are dedicated to academic research or serve as a kind of knowledge lock. They are beneficial to read, but unfortunately, there are too few of these valuable publications now.

Although there is a difference between soft and hard in terms of nature, it is best to soften the hard ones. "Historical Essays" and "Scientific Essays" are the creations of this technique. In fact, why only "history" and "science" like this? "Politics," "economics," and others can also be like this.

Since it is called a magazine, it should be diverse. But维者is not completely unsystematic, that is, it should be fresh and lively. The materials should be in response to the environment and seasons, the arrangement should be as lively as possible, and the cover插画should be changed from time to time, so that people will not feel familiar at first sight and cannot arouse interest at all.

Although soft publications are designed to please people, they will become boring after a long time. I think the soft ones can be slightly hardened, in other words, they should have knowledge-based text and pictures.

Regular publications were mostly monthly publications at first, but recently the most popular ones are semi-monthly publications, and weekly publications are determined. If the period is too long, it is like classics, if the period is too short, the length will be thin, and it will be meaningless to see it at a glance. Therefore, semi-monthly publications are more suitable for softer ones, and monthly publications are more suitable for harder ones.

Ten years ago, most of the magazines in our country could not be published on time. Now, all magazines can be published on time. Some have even been published early. But some still cannot be published on schedule, so we should strive for accuracy.

The most annoying thing about magazines is being腰斩ed. It is very disappointing for readers when the inaugural issue is published, or five or ten issues are published and then the publication is stopped.

Although there are many magazines in China recently, there are still no magazines with very substantial content. For example, Japan's "Central Public Opinion," "Gaizhao," and "New Tide" are of good quality and are truly rare. Here, I hope to concentrate people and resources to run the most ideal magazine.

I also have one last request, that is, I hope everyone will work together to run the most popular magazine, so that everyone can understand it and everyone can enjoy it, and promote the popularization of education and improve the level of culture in the most simple and interesting text.

I wonder when this little wish can be realized?

From "Chatting About Wind" to Humor 202

— Philosopher

Not long ago, I saw some news in certain newspapers saying that another humor magazine was about to be published, named "Chatting About Wind." It said that their publishing aim was based on Mr. Lin Yutang's advocacy of "humor," and that after three or four years of painstaking effort without success, "Chatting About Wind" was to complete Mr. Lin Yutang's unfinished ambition. Of course, we readers are always welcome; at the very least, it's one more publication in the barren publishing scene.

"Chatting About Wind" was published on the 25th, but we saw it on the 22nd, which is somewhat good. But what about the content? The cover is printed with Mr. Lin Yutang's original manuscript, and the opening illustration is a photograph of "Welcoming" Mr. Lin's departure from the country, and the back is again Mr. Lin's handwriting. As for the text? There is Mr. Lin's "Letter to a Friend," and the "Preface" also has endless mentions of Mr. Lin. Naturally, the final "Editor's Notes" cannot avoid mentioning Mr. Lin either. How great! Mr. Yutang!

For such a publication, which advocates leisure, is full of scholar-official airs, and exudes an air of elegance, we cannot give it a higher evaluation. But here we cannot help but mention the humor they claim to promote. I say that "humor" cannot exist as a standalone literary work. What we can acknowledge as "humor" is a style in literature. Strictly speaking, it is just a clown in literature. However, we acknowledge that "humor" is a talent, a congenital inheritance, not a learned skill, much less something that can be forced or imitated. If "humor" is a sigh from the heart in response to unbearable suffering, then it takes the current tragic situation too lightly, too superficially.

As for those who advocate "humor" and revere the late Ming dynasty's Yuan Zhonglang and Yuan Xiaoxiu, that is even more of a joke! This is nothing less than ironclad proof that they regard "humor" as the resurrection of scholar-official literature!

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

Is "Moral Degeneration" at Hand? 214

— Zi Nan

These are the years when retrogressive people shake their heads and sigh about "moral degeneration." Especially when talking about women, the old-fashioned gentlemen spare no effort to affix many complimentary titles upon them, as if China's current plight is entirely the result of the "evil deeds" committed by these "monstrous creatures."

Upon closer inspection, the way women dress now is indeed vastly different from the way the mothers of retrogressive people dressed in their time. For example, hairstyles: the mothers of retrogressive people probably always had a bun at the back of their heads, but nowadays, even if they don't get perms, young women in Shanghai have mostly adopted the "duck's bottom" style. Another example is feet: the mothers of retrogressive people had a pair of "three-inch golden lotuses," whereas most women now, even if they don't have natural feet, have long since unbound their feet and transformed them into "civilized feet." According to retrogressive people, large feet are for easier escape in times of disaster. Therefore, the increasing domestic and foreign troubles are still due to the liberation of women's feet. As for whether men's large feet are for escaping disaster? That doesn't seem to have been answered.

But in reality, even if women's clothing is different from before, their old moral concepts remain the same. For example, "Miss Wang Meili of Ningbo, aged twenty-eight, ... Seeing the woman's beauty, Xu repeatedly thought of seducing her, but she consistently ignored him. Afterward, he repeatedly sent her letters, but she did not respond. Consequently, around 9 p.m. on the 18th, Xu sent three men to her residence. The three men all claimed to be news reporters and invited her to meet Xu outside the next day. If she refused, they would disclose the details of her love affair with Xu in the newspapers, using all sorts of intimidating words. As a result, the woman became afraid and contemplated suicide..." Logically speaking, if changing one's attire meant "moral degeneration," then that Miss Wang, "aged twenty-eight," would never have "become afraid and contemplated suicide." However, she ultimately "committed suicide." -- Was it really "suicide"? No, she was killed by old moral values. Because she feared that news reporters (?) would "disclose the details of her love affair (let's assume there was a love affair!) in the newspapers," leading to "shameful exposure."

As for whether these three people claiming to be news reporters were genuine news reporters, it's impossible to say for sure because there hasn't been any follow-up. Let's just assume that there are such black sheep among news reporters. If that Miss Wang had been influenced by new ideas, she would have been unafraid to have her love affair published in the newspapers (in fact, we have never seen a respectable newspaper disclose a female worker's love affair in the newspaper). However, precisely because that Miss Wang was too deeply poisoned by old morals, considering love as a "scandalous affair" that could not be exposed, she was taken advantage of by those claiming to be news reporters, and a pure and promising young life came to an end. Using this example, we don't know how many lives have been devoured by old morals under similar circumstances.

However, retrogressive people continue to say, "Moral degeneration is at hand." It seems that the current national apathy and unwillingness to resist anything are all due to "moral degeneration."
